The chain flows from protocol-level configuration through factory creation to stream-level execution.\\n\\n### 1. **Configuration Layer (Protobuf Definitions)**\\n\\nThe HTTP connection manager configuration is defined in two versions:\\n\\n- **data-plane-api/envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto**: The current v3 configuration schema that defines the `HttpConnectionManager` message with `http_filters` field (repeated HttpFilter). Each HttpFilter contains:\\n  - `name`: Filter configuration name\\n  - `typed_config` or `config_discovery`: Filter-specific configuration\\n  - `is_optional`: Whether the filter is optional\\n  - `disabled`: Whether the filter is disabled by default\\n\\n- **data-plane-api/envoy/config/filter/network/http_connection_manager/v2/http_connection_manager.proto**: The deprecated v2 version maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\n### 2. **Factory Interfaces (envoy/http/)**\\n\\n**FilterChainFactory** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):\\n- Core abstract interface implemented by HttpConnectionManagerConfig\\n- Defines `createFilterChain()` method that takes a FilterChainManager and creates filter instances\\n- Handles both regular HTTP filters and upgrade (WebSocket) filter chains\\n\\n**FilterChainManager** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):\\n- Sink interface provided by the connection manager to the factory\\n- Allows factories to apply filter factory callbacks via `applyFilterFactoryCb()`\\n- Maintains filter context and factory information\\n\\n**FilterChainOptions** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):\\n- Configuration options for filter chain creation\\n- Provides `filterDisabled()` method to check if filters should be skipped\\n\\n**FilterFactoryCb**:\\n- Type alias for a function that takes `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks&` and creates filter instances\\n- Used to wrap filter creation logic\\n\\n**FilterChainFactoryCallbacks** (envoy/http/filter.h):\\n- Interface for actually adding filters to a stream\\n- Methods:\\n  - `addStreamDecoderFilter()`: Add decoder filter\\n  - `addStreamEncoderFilter()`: Add encoder filter  \\n  - `addStreamFilter()`: Add bidirectional filter\\n  - `addAccessLogHandler()`: Add access log handler\\n  - `dispatcher()`: Access the event dispatcher\\n\\n### 3. **Configuration Processing (FilterChainHelper)**\\n\\n**FilterChainHelper** (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h):\\n- Template class that processes filter list from configuration\\n- Methods:\\n  - `processFilters()`: Iterates through HttpFilter protobuf messages\\n  - `processFilter()`: Handles individual filter configuration\\n  - `processDynamicFilterConfig()`: Handles ECDS (Extension Config Discovery Service) filters\\n- Creates FilterConfigProvider objects that wrap filter factory callbacks\\n- Validates filter dependencies using DependencyManager\\n- Handles optional and disabled filters\\n\\n**FilterChainUtility** (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h):\\n- Utility class with static method `createFilterChainForFactories()`\\n- Iterates through pre-built FilterConfigProviderList\\n- Applies each filter factory callback to the FilterChainManager\\n- Handles missing filter configurations by injecting MissingConfigFilter\\n\\n### 4. **Configuration Implementation (HttpConnectionManagerConfig)**\\n\\n**HttpConnectionManagerConfig** (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h):\\n- Implements both `Http::FilterChainFactory` and `Http::ConnectionManagerConfig`\\n- Constructed from the HttpConnectionManager protobuf config\\n- Stores FilterFactoriesList (list of FilterConfigProvider objects)\\n- Implements `createFilterChain()` which:\\n  1. Applies filters to the provided FilterChainManager\\n\\n**HttpConnectionManagerFilterConfigFactory** (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h):\\n- Network filter factory that creates HttpConnectionManagerConfig from protobuf\\n- Called during listener/filter chain configuration\\n\\n### 5. **Runtime Filter Chain Execution (FilterManager)**\\n\\n**FilterManager** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h):\\n- Base class managing filter execution for a stream\\n- Key responsibilities:\\n  - Stores ordered lists of decoder and encoder filters\\n  - Manages filter state and iteration\\n  - Implements streaming protocol for filter interaction\\n  - Handles all HTTP events (headers, data, trailers, metadata)\\n\\n**DownstreamFilterManager** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h):\\n- Extends FilterManager for downstream (client-facing) streams\\n- Implements full filter chain execution logic\\n\\n**FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h):\\n- Implements FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interface\\n- Called by filter factory callbacks to add filters to a stream\\n- Wraps filters in ActiveStreamDecoderFilter/ActiveStreamEncoderFilter\\n- Maintains filter context for tracking which filter created it\\n\\n**createFilterChain()** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h at line 1550):\\n- Called when a new stream is created\\n- Retrieves the FilterChainFactory from HttpConnectionManagerConfig\\n- Calls factory's `createFilterChain()` method passing itself as FilterChainManager\\n- Completes with a list of filters ready for stream processing\\n\\n### 6. **Config Provider Management**\\n\\n**FilterConfigProviderManager** (envoy/filter/config_provider_manager.h):\\n- Template interface managing both static and dynamic filter config providers\\n- Methods:\\n  - Listener loads HttpConnectionManager network filter configuration\\n2. HttpConnectionManagerFilterConfigFactory parses protobuf config\\n3. FilterChainHelper processes http_filters list in configuration\\n4. For each filter, FilterChainHelper finds registered factory and creates FilterConfigProvider\\n5. All FilterConfigProviders stored in HttpConnectionManagerConfig::filter_factories_\\n\\n**Stream Creation Phase:**\\n1. New HTTP stream arrives on connection\\n2. ConnectionManagerImpl::ActiveStream created\\n3. FilterManager::createFilterChain() called\\n4. Calls HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain() (the FilterChainFactory)\\n5. HttpConnectionManagerConfig calls FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()\\n6. For each FilterConfigProvider:\\n   - Check if filter is disabled (by route or globally)\\n   - Get actual filter factory callback from provider\\n   - Call FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb() (which is FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb)\\n   - Filter factory creates filter instance and adds via FilterChainFactoryCallbacks\\n   - FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl wraps filter and adds to FilterManager's lists\\n\\n**Execution Phase:**\\n1. HTTP events flow through FilterManager\\n2. FilterManager iterates through decoder filters in order for request events\\n3. Each filter can modify data, headers, or stop iteration\\n4. Router filter determines response and initiates upstream request\\n5. FilterManager iterates through encoder filters in reverse for response events\\n\\n### 8. **Key Design Patterns**\\n\\n**Provider Pattern:** FilterConfigProvider abstracts static vs. dynamic config sources, allowing seamless config discovery\\n\\n**Callback Pattern:** FilterFactoryCb and FilterChainFactoryCallbacks use callbacks to decouple filter creation from filter management\\n\\n**Factory Pattern:** Multiple factory interfaces (FilterChainFactory, named filter factories) allow extension and customization\\n\\n**Chain of Responsibility:** Filter chain implements classic chain of responsibility with filters processing streams in order\\n\\n### 9. **Connection Between Components**\\n\\n- HttpConnectionManager proto defines configuration schema with http_filters field\\n- HttpConnectionManagerConfig implements FilterChainFactory, reading http_filters from proto\\n- FilterChainHelper processes proto http_filters list and creates FilterConfigProviders\\n- FilterConfigProviderManager manages lifetime of these providers\\n- At stream time, FilterManager calls createFilterChain() on HttpConnectionManagerConfig\\n- HttpConnectionManagerConfig uses FilterChainUtility to iterate through stored providers\\n- Each provider's factory is applied to FilterManager via FilterChainManager interface\\n- FilterManager's FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl implementation adds filters to internal lists\\n- FilterManager then executes the filter chain for all stream events\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":5,"cache_creation_input_tokens":862,"cache_read_input_tokens":62949,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":862},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"649e9545-c5f9-40bb-8811-dc253a69ea76","uuid":"ea989c97-986d-4cca-8638-91c01a5112ba"}

Each HttpFilter contains:\\n  - `name`: Filter configuration name\\n  - `typed_config` or `config_discovery`: Filter-specific configuration\\n  - `is_optional`: Whether the filter is optional\\n  - `disabled`: Whether the filter is disabled by default\\n\\n- **data-plane-api/envoy/config/filter/network/http_connection_manager/v2/http_connection_manager.proto**: The deprecated v2 version maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\n### 2. **Factory Interfaces (envoy/http/)**\\n\\n**FilterChainFactory** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):\\n- Core abstract interface implemented by HttpConnectionManagerConfig\\n- Defines `createFilterChain()` method that takes a FilterChainManager and creates filter instances\\n- Handles both regular HTTP filters and upgrade (WebSocket) filter chains\\n\\n**FilterChainManager** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):\\n- Sink interface provided by the connection manager to the factory\\n- Allows factories to apply filter factory callbacks via `applyFilterFactoryCb()`\\n- Maintains filter context and factory information\\n\\n**FilterChainOptions** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):\\n- Configuration options for filter chain creation\\n- Provides `filterDisabled()` method to check if filters should be skipped\\n\\n**FilterFactoryCb**:\\n- Type alias for a function that takes `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks&` and creates filter instances\\n- Used to wrap filter creation logic\\n\\n**FilterChainFactoryCallbacks** (envoy/http/filter.h):\\n- Interface for actually adding filters to a stream\\n- Methods:\\n  - `addStreamDecoderFilter()`: Add decoder filter\\n  - `addStreamEncoderFilter()`: Add encoder filter  \\n  - `addStreamFilter()`: Add bidirectional filter\\n  - `addAccessLogHandler()`: Add access log handler\\n  - `dispatcher()`: Access the event dispatcher\\n\\n### 3. **Configuration Processing (FilterChainHelper)**\\n\\n**FilterChainHelper** (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h):\\n- Template class that processes filter list from configuration\\n- Methods:\\n  - `processFilters()`: Iterates through HttpFilter protobuf messages\\n  - `processFilter()`: Handles individual filter configuration\\n  - `processDynamicFilterConfig()`: Handles ECDS (Extension Config Discovery Service) filters\\n- Creates FilterConfigProvider objects that wrap filter factory callbacks\\n- Validates filter dependencies using DependencyManager\\n- Handles optional and disabled filters\\n\\n**FilterChainUtility** (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h):\\n- Utility class with static method `createFilterChainForFactories()`\\n- Iterates through pre-built FilterConfigProviderList\\n- Applies each filter factory callback to the FilterChainManager\\n- Handles missing filter configurations by injecting MissingConfigFilter\\n\\n### 4. **Configuration Implementation (HttpConnectionManagerConfig)**\\n\\n**HttpConnectionManagerConfig** (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h):\\n- Implements both `Http::FilterChainFactory` and `Http::ConnectionManagerConfig`\\n- Constructed from the HttpConnectionManager protobuf config\\n- Stores FilterFactoriesList (list of FilterConfigProvider objects)\\n- Implements `createFilterChain()` which:\\n  1. Calls `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` with stored filter factories\\n  2. Handles route-based filter chain options\\n  3. Applies filters to the provided FilterChainManager\\n\\n**HttpConnectionManagerFilterConfigFactory** (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h):\\n- Network filter factory that creates HttpConnectionManagerConfig from protobuf\\n- Called during listener/filter chain configuration\\n\\n### 5. **Runtime Filter Chain Execution (FilterManager)**\\n\\n**FilterManager** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h):\\n- Base class managing filter execution for a stream\\n- Key responsibilities:\\n  - Stores ordered lists of decoder and encoder filters\\n  - Manages filter state and iteration\\n  - Implements streaming protocol for filter interaction\\n  - Handles all HTTP events (headers, data, trailers, metadata)\\n\\n**DownstreamFilterManager** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h):\\n- Extends FilterManager for downstream (client-facing) streams\\n- Implements full filter chain execution logic\\n\\n**FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h):\\n- Implements FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interface\\n- Called by filter factory callbacks to add filters to a stream\\n- Wraps filters in ActiveStreamDecoderFilter/ActiveStreamEncoderFilter\\n- Maintains filter context for tracking which filter created it\\n\\n**createFilterChain()** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h at line 1550):\\n- Called when a new stream is created\\n- Retrieves the FilterChainFactory from HttpConnectionManagerConfig\\n- Calls factory's `createFilterChain()` method passing itself as FilterChainManager\\n- Completes with a list of filters ready for stream processing\\n\\n### 6. **Config Provider Management**\\n\\n**FilterConfigProviderManager** (envoy/filter/config_provider_manager.h):\\n- Template interface managing both static and dynamic filter config providers\\n- Methods:\\n  - `createStaticFilterConfigProvider()`: Create provider for statically inlined configs\\n  - `createDynamicFilterConfigProvider()`: Create provider for ECDS-discovered configs\\n\\n**HttpFilterConfigProviderManagerImpl** (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h):\\n- Concrete implementation for downstream HTTP filters\\n- Manages FilterConfigProvider lifecycle\\n- Handles subscription to ECDS for dynamic filter updates\\n- Validates terminal filters and filter dependencies\\n\\n**UpstreamHttpFilterConfigProviderManagerImpl** (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h):\\n- Concrete implementation for upstream HTTP filters\\n- Similar functionality to downstream variant\\n\\n**DynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl** (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h):\\n- Generic implementation supporting dynamic config discovery\\n- Maintains thread-local config state\\n- Handles config updates and removals\\n- Supports default fallback configurations\\n\\n### 7. **Execution Flow**\\n\\n**Configuration Phase:**\\n1. Listener loads HttpConnectionManager network filter configuration\\n2. HttpConnectionManagerFilterConfigFactory parses protobuf config\\n3. FilterChainHelper processes http_filters list in configuration\\n4. For each filter, FilterChainHelper finds registered factory and creates FilterConfigProvider\\n5. All FilterConfigProviders stored in HttpConnectionManagerConfig::filter_factories_\\n\\n**Stream Creation Phase:**\\n1. New HTTP stream arrives on connection\\n2. ConnectionManagerImpl::ActiveStream created\\n3. FilterManager::createFilterChain() called\\n4. Calls HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain() (the FilterChainFactory)\\n5. HttpConnectionManagerConfig calls FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()\\n6. For each FilterConfigProvider:\\n   - Check if filter is disabled (by route or globally)\\n   - Get actual filter factory callback from provider\\n   - Call FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb() (which is FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb)\\n   - Filter factory creates filter instance and adds via FilterChainFactoryCallbacks\\n   - FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl wraps filter and adds to FilterManager's lists\\n\\n**Execution Phase:**\\n1. HTTP events flow through FilterManager\\n2. FilterManager iterates through decoder filters in order for request events\\n3. Each filter can modify data, headers, or stop iteration\\n4. Router filter determines response and initiates upstream request\\n5. FilterManager iterates through encoder filters in reverse for response events\\n\\n### 8. **Key Design Patterns**\\n\\n**Provider Pattern:** FilterConfigProvider abstracts static vs. dynamic config sources, allowing seamless config discovery\\n\\n**Callback Pattern:** FilterFactoryCb and FilterChainFactoryCallbacks use callbacks to decouple filter creation from filter management\\n\\n**Factory Pattern:** Multiple factory interfaces (FilterChainFactory, named filter factories) allow extension and customization\\n\\n**Chain of Responsibility:** Filter chain implements classic chain of responsibility with filters processing streams in order\\n\\n### 9. **Connection Between Components**\\n\\n- HttpConnectionManager proto defines configuration schema with http_filters field\\n- HttpConnectionManagerConfig implements FilterChainFactory, reading http_filters from proto\\n- FilterChainHelper processes proto http_filters list and creates FilterConfigProviders\\n- FilterConfigProviderManager manages lifetime of these providers\\n- At stream time, FilterManager calls createFilterChain() on HttpConnectionManagerConfig\\n- HttpConnectionManagerConfig uses FilterChainUtility to iterate through stored providers\\n- Each provider's factory is applied to FilterManager via FilterChainManager interface\\n- FilterManager's FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl implementation adds filters to internal lists\\n- FilterManager then executes the filter chain for all stream events\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
